libevent:

libevent: when a specific event occurs on a file descriptor or after a timeout

libevent: signals or regular timeouts. 
libevent:

libevent: network servers. An application just needs to call event_dispatch()
libevent: and then add or remove events dynamically without having to change
libevent: the event loop.

uzbl:
uzbl: Any program can only be really useful if it complies with the Unix
uzbl: philosophy. Web browsers are frequent violators of this principle.
uzbl: * They build in way too much things into one (complex) program, 
uzbl:   dramatically decreasing the options to do things the way you want.
